Concluded.\nSt\nD\n\354\233\220\nSeek Him not a-mong the dead!\" They beheld the emp-ty prison; Death in chains was captive led.\nLo, He goes to dwell on high; Seraphs there, before Him bending, Chant His praises in the sky.\nFair-est of the heavenly train; Ours the joy to wait be-fore Thee, Till we rise with Thee to reign.\nD\n2\n111\nRev. J. H. MARTIN.\n264\n4\nA\n1.\nOnce for all the Saviour died, Christ the Lord was crucified; Once for all he shed his blood, Bearing forth a purple flood.\n2. Once for all our sins he bore, Bought our peace for evermore; Once for all our debt he paid, Full, complete atonement made.\n3. Once for all the Saviour rose, Victor o\'er his mighty foes; With the glorious King and Head, Saints shall waken from the dead.\n4. Once for all ascending high, Thron\'d and crown\'d above the sky, There he intercedes and reigns-Praise him in triumphant\nstrains.\n3\nB\nbb\302\262\n8\nOnce for All the Saviour Died.\nLE\nREFRAIN.\n3\n113\n3\nO, believe him and be blest!
